*testing.T) {\n\tctx := context.Background()\n\tclock := clockwork.NewFakeClock()\n\n\t// Create an auth server for testing\n\tas, err := auth.NewTestAuthServer(auth.TestAuthServerConfig{\n\t\tDir: := u2f.InMemoryRegistrationStorage(as.AuthServer.Identity)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create U2F registration storage\")\n\n\tfirstChallenge, err := u2f.RegisterInit(ctx, u2f.RegisterInitParams{\n\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\tAppConfig:  *u2fConfig,\n\t\tStorage:    u2fStorage,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to initiate first device registration\")\n\n\tfirstRegResp, err := firstMockDevice.RegisterResponse(&u2f.RegisterChallenge{\n\t\tChallenge: firstChallenge.Challenge,\n\t\tAppID:     firstChallenge.AppID,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get first device registration response\")\n\n\tfirstDev, err := u2f.RegisterVerify(ctx, u2f.RegisterVerifyParams{\n\t\tDevName: firstDeviceName,\n\t\tResp: u2f.RegisterChallengeResponse{\n\t\t\tRegistrationData: firstRegResp.RegistrationData,\n\t\t\tClientData:       firstRegResp.ClientData,\n\t\t},\n\t\tStorageKey: secondDeviceName,\n\t\tResp: u2f.RegisterChallengeResponse{\n\t\t\tRegistrationData: secondRegResp.RegistrationData,\n\t\t\tClientData:       secondRegResp.ClientData,\n\t\t},\n\t\tStorageKey: devices\")\n\n\t// Test 1: Check that U2FSignRequest includes challenges for both devices\n\tt.Run(\"U2FSignRequest with multiple devices\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\t// Create auth server with anyway\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Set password for the user\n\t\terr = as.AuthServer.UpsertPassword(username, []byte(\"password\"))\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to set user password\")\n\n\t\t// Get U2F sign request (old API)\n\t\tu2fSignReq, err := as.AuthServer.U2FSignRequest(username, []byte(\"password\"))\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get U2F sign request\")\n\t\trequire.NotNil(t, u2fSignReq)\n\n\t\t// REGRESSION: This test should show that only one challenge is present\n\t\t// when multiple devices are registered. for the issue where users with multiple U2F\n// hardware tokens would only see one device presented during login, even\n// though they had registered multiple devices.\nfunc TestRegression(t *testing.T) {\n\tctx := context.Background()\n\tclock := clockwork.NewFakeClock()\n\n\t// Create an auth server for testing\n\tas, err := auth.NewTestAuthServer(auth.TestAuthServerConfig{\n\t\tDir:   t.TempDir(),\n\t\tClock: clock,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create test auth server\")\n\n\t// Enable U2F support\n\tauthPref, err := []string{\"teleport\"},\n\t\t},\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create auth preference\")\n\terr = as.AuthServer.SetAuthPreference(authPref)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to set auth preference\")\n\n\t// Create a test user\n\tuser, _, err := auth.CreateUserAndRole(as.AuthServer, \"u2f-user\", []string{\"role\"})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create user\")\n\n\tusername := user.GetName()\n\tu2fConfig, err := authPref.GetU2F()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get U2F config\")\n\n\t// Register the first U2F device\n\tfirstDeviceName := \"u2f-key-1\"\n\tfirstMockDevice, err := mocku2f.Create()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create first mock U2F device\")\n\n\t// Initiate registration for the first device\n\tu2fStorage, err := u2f.InMemoryRegistrationStorage(as.AuthServer.Identity)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create U2F registration storage\")\n\n\tfirstChallenge, err := u2f.RegisterInit(ctx, u2f.RegisterInitParams{\n\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\tAppConfig:  *u2fConfig,\n\t\tStorage:    u2fStorage,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to initiate first device registration\")\n\n\tfirstRegResp, err := firstMockDevice.RegisterResponse(&u2f.RegisterChallenge{\n\t\tChallenge: firstChallenge.Challenge,\n\t\tAppID:     firstChallenge.AppID,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get first device registration response\")\n\n\tfirstDev, err := u2f.RegisterVerify(ctx, u2f.RegisterVerifyParams{\n\t\tDevName: firstDeviceName,\n\t\tResp: u2f.RegisterChallengeResponse{\n\t\t\tRegistrationData: firstRegResp.RegistrationData,\n\t\t\tClientData:       firstRegResp.ClientData,\n\t\t},\n\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\tStorage:    u2fStorage,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to verify first device registration\")\n\trequire.NotNil(t, firstDev)\n\n\t// Register the second U2F device\n\tsecondDeviceName := \"u2f-key-2\"\n\tsecondMockDevice, err := mocku2f.Create()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create second mock U2F device\")\n\n\t// Initiate registration for the second device\n\tsecondChallenge, err := u2f.RegisterInit(ctx, u2f.RegisterInitParams{\n\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\tAppConfig:  *u2fConfig,\n\t\tStorage:    u2fStorage,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, secondChallenge.AppID,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get second device registration response\")\n\n\tsecondDev, err := u2f.RegisterVerify(ctx, u2f.RegisterVerifyParams{\n\t\tDevName: secondDeviceName,\n\t\tResp: u2f.RegisterChallengeResponse{\n\t\t\tRegistrationData: secondRegResp.RegistrationData,\n\t\t\tClientData:       secondRegResp.ClientData,\n\t\t},\n\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\tStorage:    u2fStorage,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to verify second device registration\")\n\trequire.NotNil(t, secondDev)\n\n\t// Verify both devices are registered in the system\n\tdevices, err := as.AuthServer.GetMFADevices(ctx, username)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get MFA devices\")\n\trequire.Len(t, devices, 2, \"expected exactly 2 registered U2F devices\")\n\n\t// Test 1: Verify that authentication challenge includes both devices\n\tt.Run(\"multi-device U2F challenge generation\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\tu2fAuthStorage, err := mfaAuthChallenge method\n\t\t// This simulates what happens during user login\n\t\tauthServer := as.AuthServer.(*auth.Server)\n\t\tmfaChallenge, err := authServer.GetMFAAuthenticateChallengeForTesting(ctx, username, u2fAuthStorage)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get MFA authenticate challenge\")\n\t\trequire.NotNil(t, mfaChallenge)\n\n\t\t// REGRESSION: This test demonstrates that when creating an MFA\n\t\t// authentication challenge, the server should include a challenge for\n\t\t// each registered U2F device. If only one challenge is present instead\n\t\t// of two, it indicates the bug where multiple devices are not properly\n\t\t// supported.\n\t\t//\n\t\t// Expected behavior: 2 challenges (one for each device)\n\t\t// Buggy behavior: 1 challenge (only for the first device)\n\t\trequire.Len(t, mfaChallenge.U2F, 2,\n\t\t\t\"REGRESSION: mfaAuthChallenge should create authentication challenges for all %d registered U2F devices, \"+\n\t\t\t\t\"but only %d challenge(s) were created. \"+\n\t\t\t\t\"When a user has multiple U2F tokens registered, the server must generate a challenge for each device \"+\n\t\t\t\t\"so the user can choose which device to authenticate with.\",\n\t\t\tlen(devices), len(mfaChallenge.U2F))\n\n\t\t// Verify each challenge has unique key handles and challenges\n\t\tkeyHandles := make(map[string]bool)\n\t\tfor i, ch := range mfaChallenge.U2F {\n\t\t\trequire.NotEmpty(t, ch.KeyHandle, \"challenge %d missing KeyHandle\", i)\n\t\t\trequire.NotEmpty(t, ch.Challenge, \"challenge %d missing Challenge\", i)\n\t\t\trequire.NotEmpty(t, ch.AppID, \"challenge %d missing AppID\", i)\n\n\t\t\tif keyHandles[ch.KeyHandle] {\n\t\t\t\tt.Errorf(\"duplicate key handle in challenges: %s\", ch.KeyHandle)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tkeyHandles[ch.KeyHandle] = true\n\t\t}\n\t})\n\n\t// Test 2: Verify backward compatibility with older err, \"failed to create U2F authentication storage\")\n\n\t\tauthServer := as.AuthServer.(*auth.Server)\n\t\tmfaChallenge, err := authServer.GetMFAAuthenticateChallengeForTesting(ctx, username, u2fAuthStorage)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get MFA authenticate challenge\")\n\n\t\t// For backward compatibility with pre-6.0 clients that only understand\n\t\t// a single challenge format, the embedded AuthenticateChallenge should\n\t\t// be set when U2F challenges are present\n\t\tif len(mfaChallenge.U2F) > 0 {\n\t\t\trequire.NotNil(t, mfaChallenge.AuthenticateChallenge,\n\t\t\t\t\"REGRESSION: For backward compatibility with pre-6.0 clients, \"+\n\t\t\t\t\t\"the embedded AuthenticateChallenge field must be set when U2F challenges are present\")\n\t\t}\n\t})\n\n\t// Test 3: Verify challenge storage with device IDs\n\tt.Run(\"challenge storage uses correct device IDs\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\tu2fAuthStorage, err := u2f.InMemoryAuthenticationStorage(as.AuthServer.Identity)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create U2F authentication storage\")\n\n\t\tauthServer := as.AuthServer.(*auth.Server)\n\t\tmfaChallenge, err := authServer.GetMFAAuthenticateChallengeForTesting(ctx, username, u2fAuthStorage)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get MFA authenticate challenge\")\n\n\t\t// Each challenge should be retrievable using the device ID\n\t\trequire.Len(t, mfaChallenge.U2F, 2, \"expected 2 U2F challenges\")\n\n\t\t// Verify that challenges were stored with correct device IDs\n\t\tfor i, dev := range devices {\n\t\t\tu2fDev := dev.GetU2F()\n\t\t\trequire.NotNil(t, u2fDev, \"device %d is not a U2F device\", i)\n\n\t\t\t// Try to retrieve the challenge for this device\n\t\t\t// This will fail if the challenge storage didn't properly store\n\t\t\t// challenges with device IDs\n\t\t\tchallenge, err := u2fAuthStorage.GetU2FSignChallenge(username, dev.Id)\n\t\t\trequire.NoError(t, err,\n\t\t\t\t\"REGRESSION: Failed to retrieve stored challenge for device %q. \"+\n\t\t\t\t\t\"Challenges must be stored with device IDs to support multiple devices.\",\n\t\t\t\tdev.Id)\n\t\t\trequire.NotNil(t, challenge, \"stored challenge for device %q is nil\", dev.Id)\n\t\t}\n\t})\n}\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":18,"oldLines":15,"newStart":18,"newLines":12,"lines":[" "," import (","   \"context\"","-  \"encoding/base64\"","   \"testing\"","- secondChallenge.AppID,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get second device registration response\")\n\n\tsecondDev, err := u2f.RegisterVerify(ctx, u2f.RegisterVerifyParams{\n\t\tDevName: Single-device lock-in: After registering multiple U2F tokens, attempting\n//    to log in only presents a challenge for one device\n// 2. Users cannot select which hardware token to use during authentication\n// 3. device\")\n\n\t// Initiate registration for the first device\n\tu2fRegStorage, err := u2f.InMemoryRegistrationStorage(as.AuthServer.Identity)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create U2F registration storage\")\n\n\tfirstChallenge, err := u2f.RegisterInit(ctx, u2f.RegisterInitParams{\n\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\tAppConfig:  *u2fConfig,\n\t\tStorage:    u2fRegStorage,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to initiate first device registration\")\n\n\tfirstRegResp, err := firstMockDevice.RegisterResponse(&u2f.RegisterChallenge{\n\t\tChallenge: firstChallenge.Challenge,\n\t\tAppID:     firstChallenge.AppID,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get first device registration response\")\n\n\tfirstDev, err := u2f.RegisterVerify(ctx, u2f.RegisterChallengeResponse{\n\t\t\tRegistrationData: secondRegResp.RegistrationData,\n\t\t\tClientData:       secondRegResp.ClientData,\n\t\t},\n\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\tStorage: username,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to generate challenge for device %q\", dev.Id)\n\n\t\t\t// Verify the challenge can be retrieved using the device ID\n\t\t\tretrievedChallenge, err := u2fAuthStorage.GetU2FSignChallenge(username, dev.Id)\n\t\t\trequire.NoError(t, err,\n\t\t\t\t\"REGRESSION: Failed to retrieve stored challenge for device %q. \"+\n\t\t\t\t\t\"Each device must have its own stored challenge for multi-device authentication to work correctly.\",\n\t\t\t\tdev.Id)\n\t\t\trequire.NotNil(t, retrievedChallenge)\n\t\t\trequire.Equal(t, challenge.Challenge, retrievedChallenge.Challenge,\n\t\t\t\t\"retrieved challenge does not match generated challenge for device %q\", dev.Id)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Verify we have challenges for all devices\n\t\trequire.Len(t, u2fDevices, 2,\n\t\t\t\"REGRESSION: Expected 2 U2F devices to be registered, but got %d\",\n\t\t\tlen(u2fDevices))\n\t})\n\n\t// Test 3: Verify client/server compatibility for multi-device challenges\n\tt.Run(\"U2F challenge client/server compatibility\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\tu2fAuthStorage, err := u2f.InMemoryAuthenticationStorage(as.AuthServer.Identity)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to create U2F authentication storage\")\n\n\t\tauthServer := as.AuthServer\n\t\tdevs, err := authServer.GetMFADevices(ctx, username)\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"failed to get MFA devices\")\n\n\t\t// Generate challenges\n\t\tauthChallenges :=
